<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translingual">Translingual</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Translingual"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Symbol">Symbol</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Symbol"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="mul">cat</strong></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_standard" class="extiw" title="w:International standard">international standards</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_639-2" class="extiw" title="w:ISO 639-2">ISO 639-2</a> &amp; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_639-3" class="extiw" title="w:ISO 639-3">ISO 639-3</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/language_code#English" title="language code">language code</a> for </i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_639:cat" class="extiw" title="w:ISO 639:cat"><b>Catalan</b></a><i>.</i></li></ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: English"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">kăt</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kæt/</span>, <span class="IPA">[kʰæt]</span>, <span class="IPA">[kʰæt̚]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canadian_English" class="extiw" title="w:Canadian English">Canada</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kat/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Etymology 1"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Middle_English">cat</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/catte#Middle_English" title="catte">catte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/catt#Old_English" title="catt">catt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">male cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/catte#Old_English" title="catte">catte</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">female cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/kattu" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/kattu">*kattu</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz">*kattuz</a></i>. Further etymology is unclear. 
</p>
<div class="NavFrame">
<div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left; cursor: pointer;"><span class="NavToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">show ▼</a></span>Further etymology and cognates.</div>
<div class="NavContent derivedterms ul-column-count" data-column-count="2" style="text-align: left; display: none;">
<p>The Germanic word is generally thought to be from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/cattus#Latin" title="cattus">cattus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">domestic cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (c. 350, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rutilius_Taurus_Aemilianus_Palladius" class="extiw" title="w:Rutilius Taurus Aemilianus Palladius">Palladius</a>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/catta#Latin" title="catta">catta</a></i> (c. 75 <span style="font-size:85%;">A.D.</span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martial" class="extiw" title="w:Martial">Martial</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> from an <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afroasiatic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Afroasiatic languages">Afroasiatic</a></span> language. This would roughly match how domestic cats themselves spread, as genetic studies suggest they began to spread out of the <a href="/wiki/Near_East" title="Near East">Near East</a> / <a href="/wiki/Fertile_Crescent" title="Fertile Crescent">Fertile Crescent</a> during the Neolithic (being in Cyprus by 9500 years ago,<sup id="cite_ref-ISample_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ISample-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-COttoni_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COttoni-3">[3]</a></sup> and Greece and Italy by 2500 years ago<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup>), especially after they became popular in Egypt.<sup id="cite_ref-ISample_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ISample-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-COttoni_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COttoni-3">[3]</a></sup> However, every proposed source word has presented problems. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adolphe_Pictet" class="extiw" title="w:Adolphe Pictet">Adolphe Pictet</a><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> and many subsequent sources refer to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barabra" class="extiw" title="w:Barabra">Barabra</a> (Nubian) <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="onw-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kaddîska</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and "Nouba" (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nobiin_language" class="extiw" title="w:Nobiin language">Nobiin</a>) <i class="Latn mention" lang="fia"><a href="/w/index.php?title=kad%C4%ABs&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="kadīs (page does not exist)">kadīs</a></i> as possible sources or cognates,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> but M. Lionel Bender says the Nubian word is a loan from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar"><a href="/wiki/%D9%82%D8%B7%D8%A9#Arabic" title="قطة">قِطَّة</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qiṭṭa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-Qitta_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Qitta-7">[7]</a></sup> Jean-Paul Savignac suggests the Latin word is from an Egyptian precursor of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Coptic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Coptic language">Coptic</a></span> <i class="Copt mention" lang="cop"><a href="/wiki/%CF%A3%E2%B2%81%E2%B2%A9#Coptic" title="ϣⲁⲩ">ϣⲁⲩ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cop-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šau</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tomcat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> suffixed with feminine <i class="Latn mention" lang="egy"><a href="/wiki/-t#Egyptian" title="-t">-t</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> but John Huehnergard says "the source [...] was clearly not Egyptian itself, where no analogous form is attested."<sup id="cite_ref-Qitta_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Qitta-7">[7]</a></sup>
</p><p>It may be a <a href="/wiki/Wanderwort" title="Wanderwort">Wanderwort</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> Kroonen says the word must have existed in Germanic from a very early date, as it shows morphological alternations, and suggests that it might have been borrowed from Uralic, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_S%C3%A1mi" class="extiw" title="w:Northern Sámi">Northern Sami</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="se"><a href="/w/index.php?title=ga%C4%91fe&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="gađfe (page does not exist)">gađfe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">female stoat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hungarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hungarian language">Hungarian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hu"><a href="/wiki/h%C3%B6lgy#Hungarian" title="hölgy">hölgy</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stoat; lady, bride</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Uralic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Uralic language">Proto-Uralic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="urj-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Uralic/k%C3%A4%C4%8Fw%C3%A4" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Uralic/käďwä">*käďwä</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">female (of a fur animal)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup>
</p><p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Alternative forms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catte#English" title="catte">catte</a></span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>An animal of the family <span class="biota"><a href="/wiki/Felidae#Translingual" title="Felidae">Felidae</a></span>:
<span class="nyms-toggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonyms&nbsp;▲</a></span><span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/felid#English" title="felid">felid</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/feline#English" title="feline">feline</a></span>, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">member of the subfamily <span class="biota"><a href="/wiki/Pantherinae#Translingual" title="Pantherinae">Pantherinae</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pantherine#English" title="pantherine">pantherine</a></span>, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">technically, all members of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="/wiki/Panthera#Translingual" title="Panthera"><i>Panthera</i></a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/panther#English" title="panther">panther</a></span></span></dd></dl>

Studies in various <b>cats</b> (tigers, cheetahs and domestic cats) showed that one of these genes has mutated and no longer works.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<ol><li>A domesticated <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/species#English" title="species">species</a> (<span class="biota"><a href="/wiki/Felis_catus#Translingual" title="Felis catus"><i>Felis catus</i></a></span>) of <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/feline#English" title="feline">feline</a> animal, commonly kept as a house <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pet#English" title="pet">pet</a>. <span class="defdate">[from 8<sup>th</sup>c.]</span>

<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1892</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Besant" class="extiw" title="w:Walter Besant">Walter Besant</a>, chapter II, in <cite>The Ivory Gate<span class="q-hellip-sp">&nbsp;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="A Novel">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, New York, N.Y.: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harper_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Harper (publisher)">Harper &amp; Brothers</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&nbsp;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Franklin Square">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/title/16832619">→OCLC</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">At twilight in the summer there is never anybody to fear—man, woman, or <b>cat</b>—in the chambers and at that hour the mice come out. They do not eat parchment or foolscap or red tape, but they eat the luncheon crumbs.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Any similar animal of the family <span class="biota"><a href="/wiki/Felidae#Translingual" title="Felidae">Felidae</a></span>, which includes <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/lion#English" title="lion">lions</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/tiger#English" title="tiger">tigers</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/bobcat#English" title="bobcat">bobcats</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/leopard#English" title="leopard">leopards</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cougar#English" title="cougar">cougars</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cheetah#English" title="cheetah">cheetahs</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/caracal#English" title="caracal">caracals</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/lynx#English" title="lynx">lynxes</a>, and other such non-domesticated species.

<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A sturdy merchant sailing vessel <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">now only in "<a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/catboat#English" title="catboat">catboat</a>"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> The game of <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/trap_ball#English" title="trap ball">trap ball</a>.
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> The <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/trap#English" title="trap">trap</a> in that game.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> The pointed piece of wood that is struck in the game of <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/tipcat#English" title="tipcat">tipcat</a>.</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#vulgar" title="Appendix:Glossary">vulgar</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/African-American_Vernacular_English" class="extiw" title="w:African-American Vernacular English">African-American Vernacular</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/vagina#English" title="vagina">vagina</a>, a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/vulva#English" title="vulva">vulva</a>; the female external genitalia.

<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>2007</b></span>, Franklin White, <cite>Money for Good</cite>, Simon and Schuster, page <span class="None" lang="und">64</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">I had a notion to walk over to her, rip her apron off, sling her housecoat open and put my finger inside her <b>cat</b> to see if she was wet or freshly fucked because the dream I had earlier was beginning to really annoy me.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/double#English" title="double">double</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/tripod#English" title="tripod">tripod</a> (for holding a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/plate#English" title="plate">plate</a>, etc.) with six feet, of which three rest on the ground, in whatever position it is placed.</li>
<li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English:_wheeled_shelter" data-senseid="wheeled shelter"> <span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#historical" title="Appendix:Glossary">historical</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/wheel#English" title="wheel">wheeled</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/shelter#English" title="shelter">shelter</a>, used in the <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Middle_Ages#English" title="Middle Ages">Middle Ages</a> as a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/siege#English" title="siege">siege</a> weapon to allow <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/assailant#English" title="assailant">assailants</a> to approach enemy <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/defence#English" title="defence">defences</a>.

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Translations">Translations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Translations"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<div class="pseudo NavFrame"><div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left;">See <a href="/wiki/cat/translations#Noun" title="cat/translations">cat/translations §&nbsp;Noun</a>.</div></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en s-verb-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en ing-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catting#English" title="catting">catting</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en ed-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catted#English" title="catted">catted</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/nautical#English" title="nautical">nautical</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/hoist#English" title="hoist">hoist</a> (the <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/anchor#English" title="anchor">anchor</a>) by its <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/ring#English" title="ring">ring</a> so that it hangs at the <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cathead#English" title="cathead">cathead</a>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1922</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Lynde" class="extiw" title="w:Francis Lynde">Francis Lynde</a>, <cite>Pirates' Hope</cite>, New York: Charles Scribner's Sons, page <span class="None" lang="und">226</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">The anchors were <b>catted</b> at the bows of the yacht …</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/nautical#English" title="nautical">nautical</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To flog with a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cat-o%27-nine-tails#English" title="cat-o'-nine-tails">cat-o'-nine-tails</a>.</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/vomit#English" title="vomit">vomit</a>.</li>
<li>To go <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/wander#English" title="wander">wandering</a> at <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/night#English" title="night">night</a>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1998</b></span>, Mary Spencer, <cite>Lady's Wager</cite>, page <span class="None" lang="und">324</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">"He doesn't realize that I know," Lord Callan said, "but it's been pretty obvious that most of his <b>catting</b> about London's darker alleys has been a search for his origins.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>2010</b></span>, Claude Brown, <cite>Manchild in the Promised Land</cite>, page <span class="None" lang="und">18</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">This was going to be my first try at <b>catting</b> out. I went looking for somebody to <b>cat</b> with me.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>2012</b></span>, Valerie Hansen, <cite>Wages of Sin</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">My own dear wife could have tended to his needs if she hadn't been out <b>catting</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/gossip#English" title="gossip">gossip</a> in a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/catty#English" title="catty">catty</a> manner.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1932</b></span>, Hugh Brooke, <cite>Man Made Angry</cite>, page <span class="None" lang="und">134</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">Men from young to middleaged, with matt faces, vivacious and brightly dressed, <b>catted</b> together in gay groups.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1996</b></span>, Alistair Boyle, <cite>The Unlucky Seven</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">They smiled, touched, rolled their eyes and raised their eyebrows, as they relived the audition and <b>catted</b> about some of their competition.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>2016</b></span>, Melanie Benjamin, <cite>The Swans of Fifth Avenue</cite>, page <span class="None" lang="und">293</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">In the story, Lady Ina gossiped and <b>catted</b> about a parade of the rich and famous—Jackie Kennedy looking like an exaggerated version of herself, Princess Margaret so boring she made people fall asleep, Gloria Vanderbilt so ditzy she didn't recognize her first husband.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Etymology 2"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/concatenate#English" title="concatenate">concatenate</a></i>, derived from the program's function of concatenating files. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/concat#English" title="concat">concat</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A program and command in <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Unix#English" title="Unix">Unix</a> that reads one or more files and directs their content to the standard output.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en s-verb-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en ing-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catting#English" title="catting">catting</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en ed-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catted#English" title="catted">catted</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/apply#English" title="apply">apply</a> the <b>cat</b> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/command#English" title="command">command</a> to (one or more files).</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/dump#English" title="dump">dump</a> large amounts of data on (an unprepared target), usually with no intention of browsing it carefully.</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Etymology 3"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>)</span>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#abbreviation" title="Appendix:Glossary">Abbreviation</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catapult#English" title="catapult">catapult</a></i></span></span>.

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#abbreviation" title="Appendix:Glossary">Abbreviation</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catfish#English" title="catfish">catfish</a></i></span></span>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1913</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Willa_Cather" class="extiw" title="w:Willa Cather">Willa Cather</a>, chapter 2, in <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/O_Pioneers!" class="extiw" title="s:O Pioneers!">O Pioneers!</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">She missed the fish diet of her own country, and twice every summer she sent the boys to the river, twenty miles to the southward, to fish for channel <b>cat</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1916</b></span>, M. Shults, “Fishing for Yellow Cat in the Brazos”, in <cite>Field and Stream</cite>, <span class="None" lang="und">vol. 21, 478</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">Fishing for <b>cat</b> is probably, up to a certain stage, the least exciting of all similar sports.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#abbreviation" title="Appendix:Glossary">Abbreviation</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/caterpillar#English" title="caterpillar">caterpillar</a></i></span></span>.
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> Any of a variety of earth-moving <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/machine#English" title="machine">machines</a>. (from their manufacturer <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caterpillar_Inc." class="extiw" title="w:Caterpillar Inc.">Caterpillar Inc.</a>)</li>
<li>A ground vehicle which uses <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/caterpillar_track#English" title="caterpillar track">caterpillar tracks</a>, especially tractors, trucks, minibuses, and snow groomers.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#abbreviation" title="Appendix:Glossary">Abbreviation</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/computed_axial_tomography#English" title="computed axial tomography">computed axial tomography</a></i></span></span>. Often used <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/attributively#English" title="attributively">attributively</a>, as in “<a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/CAT_scan#English" title="CAT scan">CAT scan</a>” or “<a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/CT_scan#English" title="CT scan">CT scan</a>”.</li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Indonesian">Indonesian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Indonesian"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Malay">cat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hokkien" class="extiw" title="w:Hokkien">Hokkien</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="nan-hbl"><a href="/wiki/%E6%BC%86#Hokkien" title="漆">漆</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="nan-hbl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chhat</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_2">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Alternative forms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="ga"><a href="/wiki/cut#Irish" title="cut">cut</a></span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaeltacht_Cois_Fharraige" class="extiw" title="w:Gaeltacht Cois Fharraige">Cois Fharraige</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/catt#Old_Irish" title="catt">catt</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/kattos" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/kattos">*kattos</a></i> or from <a href="/wiki/cattus" title="cattus">Latin cattus</a>, possibly even <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz">*kattuz</a></i>.  
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_3">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Munster_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Munster Irish">Munster</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aran_Islands" class="extiw" title="w:Aran Islands">Aran</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Irish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Irish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kɑt̪ˠ/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaeltacht_Iorrais_agus_Acaill" class="extiw" title="w:Gaeltacht Iorrais agus Acaill">Mayo</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ulster_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Ulster Irish">Ulster</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Irish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Irish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kat̪ˠ/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaeltacht_Cois_Fharraige" class="extiw" title="w:Gaeltacht Cois Fharraige">Cois Fharraige</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Irish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Irish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kʊt̪ˠ/</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">as if spelled <i>cut</i></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="ga">cat</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>genitive singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="ga"><a href="/wiki/cait#Irish" title="cait">cait</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="ga"><a href="/wiki/cait#Irish" title="cait">cait</a></b>)</span>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Malay">Malay</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Malay"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hokkien" class="extiw" title="w:Hokkien">Hokkien</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="nan-hbl"><a href="/wiki/%E6%BC%86#Hokkien" title="漆">漆</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="nan-hbl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chhat</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_3">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Alternative forms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/catt#Old_English" title="catt">catt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">male cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/catte#Old_English" title="catte">catte</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">female cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, this is in turn from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz">*kattuz</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Norman">Norman</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Norman"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norman" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norman">Old Northern French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Old_French">cat</a></i> (variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/chat#Old_French" title="chat">chat</a></i>) from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/cattus#Latin" title="cattus">cattus</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_6">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norman_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Norman phonology">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ka/</span></li>
<li><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r50165410"><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: middle; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">Audio (Jersey)</td><td class="audiofile"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><span class="mw-tmh-player audio mw-file-element" style="width:175px;"><audio id="mwe_player_5_placeholder" preload="none" class="" width="175" style="width:175px;" data-durationhint="1" data-mwtitle="Jer-cat.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" playsinline="" disabled="disabled" tabindex="-1"></audio><a class="mw-tmh-play" href="/wiki/File:Jer-cat.ogg" title="Play audio" role="button"><span class="mw-tmh-play-icon"></span></a><span class="mw-tmh-duration mw-tmh-label"><span class="sr-only">Duration: 1 second.</span><span aria-hidden="true">0:01</span></span></span></span></span></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:Jer-cat.ogg" title="File:Jer-cat.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nrf">cat</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nrf p-form-of" lang="nrf"><a href="/wiki/cats#Norman" title="cats">cats</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nrf"><a href="/wiki/catte#Norman" title="catte">catte</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">cat</a></span>
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <span class="None" lang="und"><b>1830</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_M%C3%A9tivier" class="extiw" title="w:George Métivier">George Métivier</a>, <cite>Lamentations de Damaris</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="nrf">Où'est donc qu'j'iron, mé et mes puches / Ma <b>catte</b>, et l'reste de l'écu?</span><dl><dd><small>(please <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Quotations#Adding_translations_to_quotations" title="Wiktionary:Quotations">add an English translation</a> of this quotation)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1903</b></span>, Edgar MacCulloch, “Proverbs, Weather Sayings, etc.”, in <cite>Guernsey Folk Lore</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/cu31924029911710/page/514/mode/1up?view=theater">[1]</a></sup>, page <span class="None" lang="und">514</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="nrf">Si ùn <b>cat</b> s'amord au lard, nou ne sairait l'en d's'amordre.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If a <b>cat</b> takes a liking for bacon, you can't break her of it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>2006</b></span>, Peggy Collenette, “D'la gâche de Guernési”, in <cite>P'tites Lures Guernésiaises</cite>, Cromwell Press, published <span class="None" lang="und">2006</span>, page <span class="None" lang="und">20</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="nrf">Ils d'visirent pour enne haeure, mais la Louise était pas chagrinaïe au tour sa pâte, pasqué a savait que le <b>cat</b> était à gardaïr la pâte caoude.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They talked for an hour, but Louise was not worried about her dough, because she knew that the <b>cat</b> was keeping the dough warm.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jersey" class="extiw" title="w:Jersey">Jersey</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:common_dab" class="extiw" title="w:en:common dab">common dab</a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Limanda_limanda" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Limanda limanda"><i>Limanda limanda</i></a></span>)</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fro">cat</strong> <span class="ib-content qualifier-content">oblique singular</span>,&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>oblique plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/caz#Old_French" title="caz">caz</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=catz&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="catz (page does not exist)">catz</a></b>, <i>nominative singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/caz#Old_French" title="caz">caz</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=catz&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="catz (page does not exist)">catz</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><strong class="selflink">cat</strong></b>)</span>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Romanian">Romanian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Romanian"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#loanword" title="Appendix:Glossary">Borrowed</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="Arab ota-Arab mention" lang="ota"><a href="/wiki/%D9%82%D8%A7%D8%AA#Ottoman_Turkish" title="قات">قات</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kat</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_7">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Romanian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Romanian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kat/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_10">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="ro">cat</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-ro p-form-of" lang="ro"><a href="/wiki/caturi#Romanian" title="caturi">caturi</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dated" title="Appendix:Glossary">dated</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/floor#English" title="floor">floor</a> (<a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/storey#English" title="storey">storey</a>)
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1892</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbu_%C8%98tef%C4%83nescu_Delavrancea" class="extiw" title="w:Barbu Ștefănescu Delavrancea">Barbu Ștefănescu Delavrancea</a>, <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ro:Domnul_Vucea" class="extiw" title="s:ro:Domnul Vucea">Mr. Vucea</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="ro">Mi-aduc bine aminte că unul sărea de la al cincilea <b>cat</b>, și c-o mână își ținea pălăria. Grozav îi era de pălărie!</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I remember well that one was jumping from the fifth <b>floor</b>, and was holding his hat with one hand. That proud was he of the hat!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Scots">Scots</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Scots"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_4">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Alternative forms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="sco"><a href="/wiki/kat#Scots" title="kat">kat</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="sco"><a href="/wiki/ket#Scots" title="ket">ket</a></span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ulster_Scots_dialects" class="extiw" title="w:Ulster Scots dialects">Ulster</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_9">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Scots" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Scots">Middle Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Scots">cat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Early_Scots" class="extiw" title="w:Early Scots">Early Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/catte#Middle_English" title="catte">catte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/catte#Middle_English" title="catte">catte</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Middle_English">cat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/catte#Old_English" title="catte">catte</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/catt#Old_English" title="catt">catt</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/kattu" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/kattu">*kattu</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz">*kattuz</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_11">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Scottish_Gaelic">Scottish Gaelic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Scottish Gaelic"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg/220px-Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="293" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg/330px-Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg/440px-Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg 2x" data-file-width="950" data-file-height="1267"></a><figcaption>Cat.</figcaption></figure>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_10">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/catt#Old_Irish" title="catt">catt</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/cattus#Latin" title="cattus">cattus</a></i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Irish language">Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Irish">cat</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manx_language" class="extiw" title="w:Manx language">Manx</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gv"><a href="/wiki/kayt#Manx" title="kayt">kayt</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_8">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Scottish_Gaelic_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Scottish Gaelic pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kʰaʰt̪/</span></li>
<li>Hyphenation: <span class="Latn" lang="gd">cat</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="gd">cat</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>genitive singular</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-gd gen|s-form-of" lang="gd"><a href="/wiki/cait#Scottish_Gaelic" title="cait">cait</a></b>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-gd p-form-of" lang="gd"><a href="/wiki/cait#Scottish_Gaelic" title="cait">cait</a></b>)</span>
